INCLUDE Irvine32.inc

.data
	prompt BYTE "Enter your",0
	pemp   BYTE " employee ID:",0
	psal   byte " salary:",0
	pname BYTE " name:",0
	pyear BYTE " year of birth:",0
	innerloop BYTE 0
	tsal    qword  0
	vname BYTE 20 dup(?)
	dmsg  byte "Salary is above 50000 and the Tax is",0
	nmdi   byte 2
	dntmsg byte "No Tax",0

.code
main PROC

		mov edx, OFFSET prompt
		call writeString
		mov edx, OFFSET pname
		call writeString
		mov edx,0
		mov edx, offset pname
		mov ecx,sizeof pname
		call readString
		call crlf

		mov edx, OFFSET prompt
		call writeString
		mov edx, OFFSET pyear
		call writeString
		mov edx,0
		mov edx, offset pyear
		mov ecx,sizeof pyear
		call readString
		call crlf

		mov edx, OFFSET prompt
		call writeString
		mov edx, OFFSET pemp
		call writeString
		mov edx,0
		mov edx, offset pemp
		mov ecx,sizeof pemp
		call readString
		call crlf

		mov edx, OFFSET prompt
		call writeString
		mov edx, OFFSET psal
		call writeString
		mov edx,0
		call readDec
		cmp eax,100
		JA L1
		JNA L2

		L1:
		mov edx,offset dmsg
		call writestring
		div nmdi
		call writedec
		exit
		L2:
		mov edx,offset dntmsg
		call writestring





			


exit
main ENDP
END main
06/10/2019, 4:00 pm - Mubasher Ansari: TITLE My First Program (Test.asm)
INCLUDE Irvine32.inc

.data

eId BYTE "Enter Your ID : ",0
eName BYTE "Enter Your Name : ",0
eYOB BYTE "Enter you year of birth : ",0
eSal BYTE "Enter Your Annual salary : ",0
id BYTE 20 DUP(?)
name1 BYTE 20 DUP(?)
yob word ?
salary dword ?
tr BYTE "Tax : ",0
fl BYTE "No Tax applicable.",0

.code
main PROC

mov edx, offset eId
call writeString
mov edx, offset id
mov ecx, 20
call readstring

mov edx, offset eName
call writeString
mov edx, offset name1
mov ecx, 20
call readstring

mov edx, offset eYOB
call writeString
mov edx, offset yob
call readDec

mov edx, offset eSal
call writeString
mov edx, offset salary
call readDec

mov ebx,50000d
cmp eax,ebx
JAE Greater
JMP notGreater

Greater:
	mov esi, 2
	mov edx, 0
	div esi
	mov edx, offset tr
	call writeString
	call writeDec
	call crlf
	
	JMP exit_pro

notGreater:
	mov edx,offset fl
	call writestring
exit_pro:
exit
main ENDP
END main

06/10/2019, 7:40 pm - Osama Fast: Include Irvine32.inc
.data
array  BYTE 15, 10, 25, 20, 30
count DWORD 5

.code
main PROC
    mov ecx,count      
    dec ecx               

outer:                
    mov ebx,ecx
    mov esi,0 

inner:

    mov al,array[si]
    mov dl,array[si+1]
    cmp al,dl

    jnc noswap 

    mov array[si],dl
    mov array[si+1],al

noswap: 
    inc si
    dec bx
    jnz inner

    loop outer
        exit        
main ENDP
END main

		  void cal()
		  {
		  	area=length*width;
		  }
		  
};
class block:public rectangle{
	public:
    int height,volume;
	void getheight()
	
	{
		cout<<"Height=";
		cin>>height;
	}
	void getdata()
	{
		rectangle::getwidth();
		rectangle::getlength();
		getheight();
	}
	void display()
	{
		rectangle::display();
		cout<<"Height is="<<height<<endl<<"Volume is="<<volume;
	}
	void cal()
	{
		volume=length*width*height;
	}
};
int main()
{
	 block b;
	 cout<<"Enter data"<<endl;
	 b.getdata();
	 b.cal();
	 b.cal();
	 cout<<"Display data"<<endl;
	 b.display();
	 
	 
}

10/11/2019, 8:55 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include <iostream.h>
#include <conio.h>
class Time
{
    int h,m,s;
    public:
    Time()
    {
        h=0, m=0; s=0;
    }
    void setTime();
    void show()
    {
        cout<< h<< ":"<< m<< ":"<< s;
    }
    
    //overloading '+' operator
    Time operator+(time);   
};

Time Time::operator+(Time t1)	//operator function
{
    Time t;
    int a,b;
    a = s+t1.s;
    t.s = a%60;
    b = (a/60)+m+t1.m;
    t.m = b%60;
    t.h = (b/60)+h+t1.h;
    t.h = t.h%12;
    return t;
}

void time::setTime()
{
    cout << "\n Enter the hour(0-11) ";
    cin >> h;
    cout << "\n Enter the minute(0-59) ";
    cin >> m;
    cout << "\n Enter the second(0-59) ";
    cin >> s;
}

void main()
{
    Time t1,t2,t3;
 
    cout << "\n Enter the first time ";
    t1.setTime();
    cout << "\n Enter the second time ";
    t2.setTime();
    t3 = t1 + t2;	//adding of two time object using '+' operator
    cout << "\n First time ";
    t1.show();
    cout << "\n Second time ";
    t2.show();
    cout << "\n Sum of times ";
    t3.show();
    getch();
}

10/11/2019, 9:14 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;
class PrimeNumber{
public:
    PrimeNumber(); //default constructor sets prime number to 1
    PrimeNumber(int numberValue); //sets the value of number to argument passed

    int getNumber() const; //returns the current value in the number

    PrimeNumber operator ++(int); //sets the value of number to next prime number
private:
    int number;
    bool isPrimeNumber(int number); //checks whether the number is prime
    int nextPrimeNumber(int number);  //returns the next prime number
};
PrimeNumber::PrimeNumber() : number(1){}
PrimeNumber::PrimeNumber(int numberValue) : number(numberValue){}

int PrimeNumber::getNumber() const{ return number; }

bool PrimeNumber::isPrimeNumber(int number){
    bool result = true;
    for(int i = 2; i<number/2; i++){
        if(number % i == 0){
            result = false;
            break;
        }
    }
    return result;
}
int PrimeNumber::nextPrimeNumber(int number){
    int next = 0;
    while(true){
        number++;
        if(isPrimeNumber(number)){
            next = number;
            break;
        }
    }
    return next;
}
PrimeNumber PrimeNumber::operator ++(int){
    PrimeNumber pn;
    pn.number = nextPrimeNumber(number);
    return pn;
}
int main(){
    PrimeNumber p(7), incremented;
    incremented = p++;
    cout << "Next prime number is: " << incremented.getNumber();
    cout << endl;
    return 0;
}

17/11/2019, 10:33 pm - Mubasher Ansari: include irvine32.inc
Gfreqs proto,tar : ptr byte, fTable : ptr DWORD,len :DWORD
.data
target BYTE "AAEBDCFBBC",0
freqTable DWORD 256 DUP(0)

.code


main proc

INVOKE Gfreqs, ADDR target, ADDR freqTable,lengthof target
exit
main endp

Gfreqs proc , tar : ptr byte, fTable : ptr DWORD,len:DWORD
    mov ecx,len
    mov esi,tar
    mov bl,4
    L1:
    
    mov eax,0
    lodsb
    mul bl
    mov edi,fTable
    add edi,eax
    inc DWORD ptr [edi]
    Loop l1

    mov ecx,256
    mov esi,fTable
    mov edi,0
    L2:
        mov eax,edi
        call writeDec
        mov eax,32
        call writeChar
        lodsd
        call writeDec
        call crlf
        inc edi
        loop l2
    ret
Gfreqs endp
end main

25/11/2019, 6:12 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include<iostream>
	#include<conio.h> 
	#include<fstream>
	using namespace std;
	class student{
		int roll;
		char name[20];
		float marks;
		void get_data(){
			cout<<"ENTER ROLL NO: ";
			cin>>roll;
			cout<<"ENTER NAME: ";
			cin>>name;
			cout<<"ENTER MARKS: ";
			cin>>marks;
		}
		void put_data(){
			cout<<"\n\t"<<roll<<"\t"<<name<<"\t"<<marks;
		}
		public:
			void addrecord(){
				fstream f;
				student st;
				f.open("student.dat",ios::app | ios::binary);
				st.get_data();
				f.write((char *)&st,sizeof(student));
				f.close();
			}
			void display(){
				fstream f;
				student st;
				f.open("student.dat",ios::in | ios::binary);
				cout<<"\n\tROLL\tNAME\t  MARKS"<<endl;
				while((f.read((char *)&st,sizeof(student)))!=NULL)
				st.put_data();
				f.close();
			}
			void search_data(){
				int temp;
				cout<<"Enter Roll no. to search: "<<endl;
				cin>>temp;
				fstream f;
				f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
				f.seekg(0,ios::beg);
				while(f.read((char *)this,sizeof(student))){
				if(temp==roll)
					{
						cout<<"Student name is: "<<name<<endl;
						cout<<"Student marks are: "<<marks<<endl;
					}
				}
				f.close();
				getch();
			}
			void del_data(){
	  			ifstream f("student.dat",ios::in);
				ofstream temp("temp.dat",ios::out|ios::app);
				int no; 
				char found='f',confirm='n';
				cout<<"Enter ROLLNO of student whose record is to be deleted. \n";
				cin>>no;
				while(!f.eof())
			{
				f.read((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				if(roll==no)
				{
					found='t';
					cout<<"are you sure want to delete this record(y/n)";
					cin>>confirm;
				if(confirm=='n')
					temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				}
				else
				temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				}
				if(found=='f'){
				cout<<"record not found!!\n";
				}
				f.close();
				temp.close();
				remove("student.dat");
				rename("temp.dat","student.dat");
				f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
				cout<<"\tDELETED! \n";
				while(!f.eof()){
				f.read((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				if(f.eof())
				break;
			}
			f.close();
			getch();
		}
		void edit_data(){
			int temp1;
			ifstream f("student.dat",ios::in);
			ofstream temp("temp.dat",ios::out|ios::app);
			cout<<"Enter Roll no. to edit: "<<endl;
			cin>>temp1;
			while(f.read((char *)this,sizeof(student))){
				if(temp1==roll)
				{
					int m;
					cout<<"Enter Updated Marks: "<<endl;
					cin>>m;
					marks=m;
					cout<<"\n\t"<<roll<<"\t"<<name<<"\t"<<marks;
					temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
					
				}
				else
				{
					temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				}
				f.close();
					temp.close();
					remove("student.dat");					
					rename("temp.dat","student.dat");
//					f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
//					while(!f.eof()){
//					f.read((char*)this,sizeof(student));
//					if(f.eof())
//					break;
				
			}
			}
//			f.close();
//			getch();
//		}	
};
int main(){
	int i;
	student s;
	do{
	cout<<"\n\tT add record press 1!\n\tTo display record press 2!\n\tTo search record press 3!\n\tTo delete record press 4!\n\tTo edit record press 5!\n\tTo exit press 0!\n "<<endl;
	cin>>i;
	if (i==1){
		s.addrecord();
	}
	else if(i==2){
		s.display();
	}
	else if(i==3){
		s.search_data();
	}
	else if(i==4){
		s.del_data();
	}
	else if(i==5){
		s.edit_data();
	}
	}while(i!=0);
}

#include<conio.h> 
#include<fstream>
using namespace std;
class student{
	int roll;
	char name[20];
	float marks;
	void get_data(){
		cout<<"ENTER ROLL NO: ";
		cin>>roll;
		cout<<"ENTER NAME: ";
		cin>>name;
		cout<<"ENTER MARKS: ";
		cin>>marks;
	}
	void put_data(){
		cout<<"\n\t|"<<roll<<"\t|"<<name<<"\t\t|"<<marks;
	}
	public:
		void addrecord(){
			fstream f;
			student st;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::app);
			st.get_data();
			f.write((char *)&st,sizeof(student));
			f.close();
		}
		void display(){
			fstream f;
			student st;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
			cout<<"\n\tROLL\tNAME\t\tMARKS"<<endl;
			while((f.read((char *)&st,sizeof(student)))!=NULL)
			st.put_data();
			f.close();
		}
		void search_data(){
			int temp;
			cout<<"Enter Roll no. to search: "<<endl;
			cin>>temp;
			fstream f;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
			while(f.read((char *)this,sizeof(student))){
			if(temp==roll)
				{
					cout<<"Student name is: "<<name<<endl;
					cout<<"Student marks are: "<<marks<<endl;
				}
			}
			f.close();
			getche();
		}
		void del_data(){
  			ifstream f("student.dat",ios::in);
			ofstream temp("temp.dat",ios::out|ios::app);
			int no; 
			char found='f',confirm='n';
			cout<<"Enter ROLLNO of student whose record is to be deleted. \n";
			cin>>no;
			while(!f.eof())
			{
				f.read((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				if(roll==no)
				{
					found='t';
					cout<<"are you sure want to delete this record(y/n)";
					cin>>confirm;
				if(confirm=='n')
					temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				}
				else
				temp.write((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				}
				if(found=='f'){
				cout<<"record not found!!\n";
				}
				f.close();
				temp.close();
				remove("student.dat");
				rename("temp.dat","student.dat");
				f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
				cout<<"\tDELETED! \n";
				while(!f.eof()){
				f.read((char*)this,sizeof(student));
				if(f.eof())
				break;
			}
			f.close();
			getche();
		}
		void edit_data(){
			student std,std1;
			int temp1;
			ifstream f("student.dat",ios::in);
			ofstream temp("temp.dat",ios::out);
			cout<<"Enter Roll no. to edit: "<<endl;
			cin>>temp1;
			while(f.read((char*)&std,sizeof(student))){
				
				if(temp1==std.roll)
				{
					cout<<"Enter Updated Marks: "<<endl;
					cin>>std.marks;
					cout<<"\n\t"<<std.roll<<"\t"<<std.name<<"\t"<<std.marks;
					temp.write((char*)&std,sizeof(student));
					
				}
				else
				{
					temp.write((char*)&std,sizeof(student));
				}
			}
			f.close();
			temp.close();
			ifstream tempFile("temp.dat",ios::in);
			
			while((tempFile.read((char *)&std,sizeof(student)))!=NULL)
			{
				cout<<std.roll<<" "<<std.name<<" "<<std.marks<<endl;
			}
			tempFile.close();
			remove("student.dat");					
			rename("temp.dat","student.dat");
		}
		getch();
};

int main(){
	int i;
	student s;
	do{
	cout<<"\n\n\n\tTo add record press 1!\n\tTo display record press 2!\n\tTo search record press 3!\n\tTo delete record press 4!\n\tTo edit record press 5!\n\tTo exit press 0!\n "<<endl;
	cin>>i;
	if (i==1){
		s.addrecord();
	}
	else if(i==2){
		s.display();
	}
	else if(i==3){
		s.search_data();
	}
	else if(i==4){
		s.del_data();
	}
	else if(i==5){
		s.edit_data();
	}
	}while(i!=0);
}

04/12/2019, 11:36 pm - Osama Fast: #include<iostream>
#include<conio.h> 
#include<fstream>
using namespace std;
class student{
	int gst;
	string city;
	//float marks;
	void get_data(){
		cout<<"ENTER City: ";
		cin>>city;
		cout<<"ENTER GST: ";
		cin>>gst;
	}
	void put_data(){
		cout<<"\n\t|"<<city<<"\t|"<<gst;
	}
	public:
		void addrecord(){
			fstream f;
			student st;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::app);
			st.get_data();
			f.write((char *)&st,sizeof(student));
			f.close();
		}
		void display(){
			fstream f;
			student st;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
			cout<<"\n\tCity\tGST"<<endl;
			while((f.read((char *)&st,sizeof(student)))!=NULL)
			st.put_data();
			f.close();
		}
		void search_data(){
			string temp;
			cout<<"Enter City To search: "<<endl;
			cin>>temp;
			fstream f;
			f.open("student.dat",ios::in);
			while(f.read((char *)this,sizeof(student))){
			if(temp==city)
				{
					cout<<"City name is: "<<city<<endl;
					cout<<"City GST is: "<<gst<<endl;
				}
			}
			f.close();
			getche();
		}

					inp>>r;
					x++;
					if(x==1)
					{
						row=r;
					}
					if(x==2)
					{
						col=r;
					}
				}
			}
			sol[row][col];
			cout<<row<<" "<<col<<endl;
			data=new char*[row];
			for(int i=0;i<row;i++){
				*(data+i)=new char[col];
				for(int j=0;j<col;j++){
					*(*(data+i)+j)=0;
				}
			}
			for(int i=0;i<row;i++){
				for(int j=0;j<col;j++){	
					inp>>c;
					*(*(data+i)+j)=c;
				}
			}
			inp.close();

31/03/2020, 3:20 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include<iostream>
#include<fstream>
#include<cmath>
#define MAX 1000
bool find();
bool solve(int x,int y);
void show();
void show2();
bool valid(int x,int y);
using namespace std;
char **data;
int row,col;
char sol[100][100];

class Stack{
	int top;
	public:
	int a[MAX];
	Stack(){
		top=-1;
	}
	bool push(int x);
	int pop();
	int peek();
	bool isEmpty();
	void show3();
};
void Stack::show3(){
	int k=top,a[top],flag;
	flag=top;
	flag++;
	flag=flag/2;
	for(int i=0;i<k+1;i++){
		a[i]=pop();
	}
	int j=k;
	cout<<endl;
	for(int i=k;i>=flag;i--){
		cout<<"("<<a[j]<<","<<a[j-1]<<")"<<endl;
		j=j-2;
	}
}
bool Stack::push(int x){
	if(top>=(MAX-1)){
		cout<<"Stack Overflow";
		return false;
	}
	else{
	a[++top]=x;
	return true;
	}
}
int Stack::pop(){
	if(top<0){
		cout<<"Stack Underflow";
		return 0;
	}
	else{
	int x=a[top--];
	return x;
	}
}
int Stack::peek(){
	if(top<0){
	cout<<"Stack is Empty";
	return 0;
	}
	else{
		int x=a[top];
		return x;
	}
}
bool Stack::isEmpty(){
	return(top<0);
}

Stack s;
int main(){
		int r,flag=0;
		char c;
		fstream f1("input1.txt");
		if(!f1){
			cout<<"file not found!"<<endl;
			exit(1);
		}
		for(int i=0;i<1;i++){
			for(int j=0;j<2;j++){
				f1>>r;
				flag++;
				if(flag==1){
					row=r;
				}
				if(flag==2){
					col=r;
				}
			}

      cout<<"no path!";

bool solve(int x,int y){
   if(x==row-1 && y==col-1){
      {
	  sol[x][y]='-';
	  s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
	  }
      return true;
   }
   if(valid(x,y)==true){
     {
	   sol[x][y]='-';
      s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
  	 }
	if(solve(x+1,y)==true)
        return true;
      
	if(solve(x,y+1)==true)
        return true;
    
    else{
      sol[x][y]='*';
      s.pop();
      s.pop();
      return false;
   }
   return false;
}
}

   if((x>=0 && x<row && y>=0 && y<col ) && (data[x][y]=='-' || data[x][y]=='S' || data[x][y]=='E' ))
   {
		return true;
   }
   else
    return false;
}

class Stack{
	int top;
	public:
	int a[MAX];
	Stack(){
		top=-1;
	}
	bool push(int x);
	int pop();
	int peek();
	bool isEmpty();
	void show3();
};
void Stack::show3(){
	int k=top,a[top],flag;
	flag=top;
	flag++;
	flag=flag/2;
	for(int i=0;i<k+1;i++){
		a[i]=pop();
	}
	int j=k;
	cout<<endl;
	for(int i=k;i>=flag;i--){
		cout<<"("<<a[j]<<","<<a[j-1]<<")"<<endl;
		j=j-2;
	}
}
bool Stack::push(int x){
	if(top>=(MAX-1)){
		cout<<"Stack Overflow";
		return false;
	}
	else{
	a[++top]=x;
	return true;
	}
}
int Stack::pop(){
	if(top<0){
		cout<<"Stack Underflow";
		return 0;
	}
	else{
	int x=a[top--];
	return x;
	}
}
int Stack::peek(){
	if(top<0){
	cout<<"Stack is Empty";
	return 0;
	}
	else{
		int x=a[top];
		return x;
	}
}
bool Stack::isEmpty(){
	return(top<0);
}

bool find(){
   if(solve(0,0)=='*'){
      cout<<"no path!";
      return false;
   }
   return true;
}

bool solve(int x,int y){
	//check[x][y]=0;
	//cout<<"("<<x<<","<<y<<")"<<endl;
   if(data[x][y]=='E'){
      {
	  sol[x][y]='-';
	  s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
	  }
      return true;
   }
   if(valid(x,y)==true){
     
     //	cout<<"("<<x<<","<<y<<")"<<endl;
	   sol[x][y]='-';
      s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
      check[x][y]=0;
  	 
	if(solve(x+1,y)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
	else if(solve(x,y+1)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
     else if(solve(x,y-1)==true)
     {
	  return true;  
}
    else if(solve(x-1,y)==true)
    {
       return true;
}
    else{
      sol[x][y]='*';
     check[x][y]=1;
      s.pop();
      s.pop();
      return false;
   }
   return false;
}
}

bool valid(int x,int y){
	//cout<<"("<<x<<","<<y<<")"<<endl;
   if((x>=0 && x<row && y>=0 && y<col ) && (data[x][y]=='-' || data[x][y]=='S' || data[x][y]=='E' )&& CheckVisited(check,x,y)==true)
   {
  // 	cout<<"True"<<endl;
		return true;
   }
   else
    return false;
}

	ofstream f2("output1.txt");
    for(int i=0;i<row;i++){
      for(int j=0;j<col;j++)
      	if(sol[i][j] == '-'){
      		cout<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;      		
      		f2<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;
		  }
   }
   f2.close();
}

#include<fstream>
using namespace std;
int main()
{
	int n,queries,c,Counter;
	fstream inp("A1.txt");
	if(!inp)
	{
		cout<<"FIle not Exist"<<endl;
	    exit(1);	
	}
	inp>>n;
	if(n>30000)
	{
		ofstream  out("Output.txt");
		out<<"Error In Input-------"<<endl;
		exit(1);
	}
	long a[n];
     for(int b=0;b<n;b++)
     {
     	inp>>c;
     	
     	a[b]=c;
	 }
	inp>>queries;
	int i,j,k,fv[queries],sv[queries],tv[queries];
	ofstream  out("Output.txt");
	for(int b=0;b<queries;b++){
		inp>>fv[b]>>sv[b]>>tv[b];
		if(fv[b]<0||sv[b]<fv[b]||sv[b]>n)
		{
			out<<fv[b]<<endl<<sv[b]<<endl<<tv[b];
			out<<"Error In Input-------"<<endl;
			exit(1);
		}
	}
	for(int b=0;b<queries;b++)
	{
		Counter=0;
		i=fv[b];j=sv[b];k=tv[b];
		while(i<j||i==j)
		{	
				if(a[i]>k)
				{	
					Counter++;
				}
				i++;
		}
     out<<Counter<<endl;
	}
}

	}
	long *data =new long[n];
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		*(data+i)=0;
	}
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		f1>>nums;
		if(!(nums>=1 && nums<=10000000000)){
			cout<<"value is not in range!"<<endl;
			exit(1);
		}
		else
		*(data+i)=nums;
	}
	cout<<n<<"\nelements are: "<<endl;
	for(i=0;i<n;i++)
	{
		cout<<*(data+i)<<endl;
	}
	f1>>t;
	check(f1,t,data,n);
	f1.close();
}
void check(istream& f1,int t,long data[],long n){
	cout<<t<<endl;
	int i=0,j,k;
	int *result=new int[t];
	for(int l1=0;l1<t;l1++){
		result[l1]=0;
		f1>>i>>j>>k;
		if(!(i>=0 && i<=j && j<=n)){
		cout<<"\n	ERROR!";
		exit(1);
		}
		for(int l2=i;l2<=j;l2++){
			if(data[l2] > k){
				result[l1]++;
			}
		}
	}
	show(result,t);
}
void show(int result[],int t){
	ofstream f2("output2.txt");
	cout<<endl<<"output file:"<<endl;
	for(int i=0;i<t;i++){
	cout<<result[i]<<endl;
	f2<<result[i]<<endl;
	}
	f2.close();
}

31/03/2020, 9:46 pm - Osama Fast: #include <iostream>
#include<string.h>
#include<fstream>
using namespace std;
class node{

 public:
 int x,y;
  int mov=0;      
 node *link;
 node *top;
 node(){
 link=NULL;
 x=0;
 }
 node(int i, node *in) {
 x = i;
 link = in;
 
 }

 node(int i){
 x=i;
 link=NULL;
 }
 node(int i,int j)
 {
 	x=i;
 	y=j;
 	link=NULL;
 	mov=-1;
 }
};
class list
{
 private:
 node *head=NULL, *tail=NULL,*top=NULL;
           
           

     
 public:
 list(){
 head=NULL;
 tail=NULL;
 }
 void push(int x,int y,int m) 
{ 
     node *temp; 
    temp = new node(); 
    if (!temp) { 
        cout << "\nHeap Overflow"; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    temp->x = x; 
     temp->y=y;
     temp->mov=m;
       temp->link = top; 
    top = temp; 
} 
int isEmpty() 
{ 

    return top == NULL; 
} 
  
  int peekx()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->x;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
  int peeky()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->y;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
  int peekm()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->mov;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
node peek() 
{ 
    if (!isEmpty()) 
        return *top; 
    else
        exit(1); 
} 
  
void pop() 
{ 
 
    if (top == NULL) { 
        cout << "\nStack Underflow" << endl; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    else { 
        top = top->link; 
 
    } 
} 
  
void display()  
{ 

	ofstream  out("Output.txt");
     node* temp; 
     list s3;
    if (top == NULL) { 
        cout << "\nStack Underflow"; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    else { 
        temp = top; 
        while (temp != NULL) {  
            s3.push(temp->x,temp->y,temp->mov);
            temp = temp->link; 
        } 
    } 
        temp = s3.top; 
        while (temp != NULL) {  
            out<< "("<< temp->x << ","<<temp->y<<")"<<endl; 
            temp = temp->link; 
        } 
} 
  

};

bool CheckVisited(int **check,int x,int y)
{
	if(check[x][y]==true)
	{
		return true;
	}
	else 
	{
		return false;
	}
}

bool SolveMaze(char **a,int row,int col,int x,int y)
{
	    int  **check;
	    	check=new int*[row];
     for(int i=0;i<row;i++)
     {
     	*(check+i)=new int[col];
     	for(int j=0;j<col;j++)
     	{
     			*(*(check+i)+j)=1;
		 }
	 }
	list s1,s2;
	int x_cord,y_cord;
	node *temp;
	s1.push(x,y,-1);
	check[x][y]=0;
	while(!s1.isEmpty())
	{
		
		int m=s1.peekm();
		m++;
		
		x_cord=s1.peekx();
		y_cord=s1.peeky();
	 	s1.pop();
		s1.push(x_cord,y_cord,m);
	    if(a[x_cord][y_cord]=='e')
		{
		   s1.display();
		    exit(1);
		}
	
	 		if(x_cord-1>=0&& (a[x_cord-1][y_cord]=='-'||a[x_cord-1][y_cord]=='e') && x_cord-1<=row-1 &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord-1,y_cord)==true)
		{
			check[x_cord-1][y_cord]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord-1,y_cord,-1);
		}

		if(x_cord+1>=0 && x_cord+1<=row-1 && (a[x_cord+1][y_cord]=='-'||a[x_cord+1][y_cord]=='e') &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord+1,y_cord)==true)
		{
			check[x_cord+1][y_cord]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord+1,y_cord,-1);
			}
	  	if(y_cord-1>=0&& (a[x_cord][y_cord-1]=='-'||a[x_cord][y_cord-1]=='e') && y_cord-1<=col-1 && CheckVisited(check,x_cord,y_cord-1)==true)
		{
	     	check[x_cord][y_cord-1]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord,y_cord-1,-1);
		}

		if(y_cord+1>=0&& (a[x_cord][y_cord+1]=='-'||a[x_cord][y_cord+1]=='e') && y_cord+1<=col-1 && CheckVisited(check,x_cord,y_cord+1)==true)
		{
         	check[x_cord][y_cord+1]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord,y_cord+1,-1);

		}
		else
		{
			check[x_cord][y_cord]=true;
			s1.pop();
		}
	}
	ofstream  out("Output.txt");
	out<<"NO path found";
	return false;
}


     
int main()
{   
          int rows,cols,y,z;
     char **input,c;
     int r,x=0;
			int count=0;
			fstream inp("Input.txt");
			if(!inp)
			{
				cout<<"file not found"<<endl;
				exit(1);
			}
            inp>>rows>>cols;
    input=new char*[rows];
     for(int i=0;i<rows;i++)
     {
     		*(input+i)=new char[cols];
     	for(int j=0;j<cols;j++)
     	{
     		inp>>c;
     		if(c=='s')
     		{
     			y=i;
     			z=j;
			 }
     		*(*(input+i)+j)=c;
  		 }
	 }
	 SolveMaze(input,rows,cols,y,z);
	return 0;
}

bool SolveMaze(char **a,int row,int col,int x,int y)
{
	    int  **check;
	    	check=new int*[row];
     for(int i=0;i<row;i++)
     {
     	*(check+i)=new int[col];
     	for(int j=0;j<col;j++)
     	{
     			*(*(check+i)+j)=1;
		 }
	 }
	list s1,s2;
	int x_cord,y_cord;
	node *temp;

	check[x][y]=0;

	{

		m++;
		
		x_cord=s1.peekx();
		y_cord=s1.peeky();
	 	s1.pop();

	    if(a[x_cord][y_cord]=='e')
		{
		   s1.display();
		    exit(1);
		}
	
	  if(m==0)
	  {
	 		if(x_cord-1>=0&& (a[x_cord-1][y_cord]=='-'||a[x_cord-1][y_cord]=='e') && x_cord-1<=row-1 &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord-1,y_cord)==true)
		{
			check[x_cord-1][y_cord]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord-1,y_cord,-1);
		}

	}
	        
	  else if(m==1)
	  {
	
		if(x_cord+1>=0 && x_cord+1<=row-1 && (a[x_cord+1][y_cord]=='-'||a[x_cord+1][y_cord]=='e') &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord+1,y_cord)==true)

06/04/2020, 8:29 pm - Osama Fast: #include <iostream>
#include<string.h>
#include<fstream>
using namespace std;
int iter=1;
class node{

 public:
 int x,y;
  int mov=0;      
 node *link;
 node *top;
 node(){
 link=NULL;
 x=0;
 }
 node(int i, node *in) {
 x = i;
 link = in;
 
 }

 node(int i){
 x=i;
 link=NULL;
 }
 node(int i,int j)
 {
 	x=i;
 	y=j;
 	link=NULL;
 	mov=-1;
 }
};
class list
{
 private:
 node *head=NULL, *tail=NULL,*top=NULL;
           
           

     
 public:
 list(){
 head=NULL;
 tail=NULL;
 }
 void push(int x,int y,int m) 
{ 
     node *temp; 
    temp = new node(); 
    if (!temp) { 
        cout << "\nHeap Overflow"; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    temp->x = x; 
     temp->y=y;
     temp->mov=m;
       temp->link = top; 
    top = temp; 
} 
int isEmpty() 
{ 

    return top == NULL; 
} 
  
  int peekx()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->x;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
  int peeky()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->y;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
  int peekm()
  {
  	if(!isEmpty())
  	{
  		return top->mov;
	  }
	  else 
	  exit(1);
  }
node peek() 
{ 
    if (!isEmpty()) 
        return *top; 
    else
        exit(1); 
} 
  
void pop() 
{ 
 
    if (top == NULL) { 
        cout << "\nStack Underflow" << endl; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    else { 
        top = top->link; 
 
    } 
} 
  
void display()  
{ 

	ofstream  out("Output.txt");
     node* temp; 
     list s3;
    if (top == NULL) { 
        cout << "\nStack Underflow"; 
        exit(1); 
    } 
    else { 
        temp = top; 
        while (temp != NULL) {  
            s3.push(temp->x,temp->y,temp->mov);
            temp = temp->link; 
        } 
    } 
        temp = s3.top; 
        while (temp != NULL) {  
            out<< "("<< temp->x << ","<<temp->y<<")"<<endl; 
            temp = temp->link; 
        } 
} 
  

};

bool CheckVisited(int **check,int x,int y)
{
	if(check[x][y]==true)
	{
		return true;
	}
	else 
	{
		return false;
	}
}

bool SolveMaze(char **a,int row,int col,int x,int y,string array)
{
	    int  **check;
	    	check=new int*[row];
     for(int i=0;i<row;i++)
     {
     	*(check+i)=new int[col];
     	for(int j=0;j<col;j++)
     	{
     			*(*(check+i)+j)=1;
		 }
	 }
	list s1,s2;
	int x_cord,y_cord;
	node *temp;
	s1.push(x,y,-1);
	check[x][y]=0;
	while(!s1.isEmpty())
	{
		//cout<<"IN WHILe"<<endl;
		int m=s1.peekm();
		m++;
		
		x_cord=s1.peekx();
		y_cord=s1.peeky();
	 	s1.pop();
		s1.push(x_cord,y_cord,m);
	    if(x_cord==row-1&&y_cord==col-1)
		{
		   s1.display();
		    exit(1);
		}
	
	  if(m==0)
	  {
	         cout<<"M==0"<<endl;  	
	 		if(x_cord-1>=0&& (a[x_cord-1][y_cord]==array[iter]) && x_cord-1<=row-1 &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord-1,y_cord)==true)
		{
			
			cout<<x_cord-1<<y_cord<<endl;
			iter++;
			check[x_cord-1][y_cord]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord-1,y_cord,-1);
		
		}

	}
	        
	  else if(m==1)
	  {
	
	   
		if(x_cord+1>=0 && x_cord+1<=row-1 && (a[x_cord+1][y_cord]==array[iter]) &&CheckVisited(check,x_cord+1,y_cord)==true)
		{
		    cout<<x_cord-1<<y_cord<<endl;
			iter++;
			check[x_cord+1][y_cord]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord+1,y_cord,-1);
			
			}

	}
	  else if(m==2)
	  {
	  	if(y_cord-1>=0&& (a[x_cord][y_cord-1]==array[iter]) && y_cord-1<=col-1 && CheckVisited(check,x_cord,y_cord-1)==true)
		{
			cout<<x_cord-1<<y_cord<<endl;
			iter++;
	     	check[x_cord][y_cord-1]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord,y_cord-1,-1);
		}
	}
	else if(m==3)
	{
		if(y_cord+1>=0&& (a[x_cord][y_cord+1]==array[iter]) && y_cord+1<=col-1 && CheckVisited(check,x_cord,y_cord+1)==true)
		{
			cout<<x_cord-1<<y_cord<<endl;
			iter++;
         	check[x_cord][y_cord+1]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord,y_cord+1,-1);

		}
	}
	else if(m==4)
	{
		cout<<"M==4"<<endl;
		cout<<x_cord+1<<y_cord+1<<endl<<a[x_cord+1][y_cord+1]<<endl<<array[iter]<<endl;
		if(y_cord+1>=0&& (a[x_cord+1][y_cord+1]==array[iter]) && y_cord+1<=col-1 && CheckVisited(check,x_cord,y_cord+1)==true)
		{
		    cout<<x_cord-1<<y_cord<<endl;
			iter++;
			check[x_cord+1][y_cord+1]=false;
			s1.push(x_cord+1,y_cord+1,-1);
		}
	}
		else
		{
			check[x_cord][y_cord]=true;
			s1.pop();
		}
	}
	ofstream  out("Output.txt");
	out<<"NO path found";
	return false;
}

06/04/2020, 8:46 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include<iostream>
#include<fstream>
#include<cmath>
#define MAX 1000
bool find();

using namespace std;
char **data;
int  **check;
int row,col;
char sol[100][100];

class Stack{
	int top;
	public:
	int a[MAX];
	Stack(){
		top=-1;
	}
	bool push(int x);
	int pop();
	int peek();
	bool isEmpty();
	void show3();
};
void Stack::show3(){
	ofstream f2("output1.txt");
	int k=top,a[top],flag;
	flag=top;
	flag++;
	flag=flag/2;
	for(int i=0;i<k+1;i++){
		a[i]=pop();
	}
	int j=k;
	cout<<endl;
	for(int i=k;i>=flag;i--){
		cout<<"("<<a[j]<<","<<a[j-1]<<")"<<endl;
		f2<<"("<<a[j]<<","<<a[j-1]<<")"<<endl;
		j=j-2;
	}
	f2.close();
}
bool Stack::push(int x){
	if(top>=(MAX-1)){
		cout<<"Stack Overflow";
		return false;
	}
	else{
	a[++top]=x;
	return true;
	}
}
int Stack::pop(){
	if(top<0){
		cout<<"Stack Underflow";
		return 0;
	}
	else{
	int x=a[top--];
	return x;
	}
}
int Stack::peek(){
	if(top<0){
	cout<<"Stack is Empty";
	return 0;
	}
	else{
		int x=a[top];
		return x;
	}
}
bool Stack::isEmpty(){
	return(top<0);
}

bool find(){
   if(solve(0,0)=='*'){
      cout<<"no path!";
      return false;
   }
   return true;
}

bool solve(int x,int y){
   if(data[x][y]=='E'){
      {
	  sol[x][y]='-';
	  s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
	  }
      return true;
   }
   if(valid(x,y)==true){
	   sol[x][y]='-';
      s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
      check[x][y]=0;
  	 
	if(solve(x+1,y)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
	else if(solve(x,y+1)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
     else if(solve(x,y-1)==true)
     {
	  return true;  
}
    else if(solve(x-1,y)==true)
    {
       return true;
}
    else{
      sol[x][y]='*';
     check[x][y]=1;
      s.pop();
      s.pop();
      return false;
   }
   return false;
}
}

bool valid(int x,int y){
   if((x>=0 && x<row && y>=0 && y<col ) && (data[x][y]=='-' || data[x][y]=='S' || data[x][y]=='E' )&& (CheckVisited(check,x,y)==true))
   {
		return true;
   }
   else
    return false;
}

	ofstream f2("output1.txt");
    for(int i=0;i<row;i++){
      for(int j=0;j<col;j++)

      		cout<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;      		
      		f2<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;
		  }
   }
   f2.close();
}

			}
			cout<<endl;
		}
	    check=new int*[4];
     	for(int i=0;i<4;i++){
     		*(check+i)=new int[4];
     		for(int j=0;j<4;j++){
     			*(*(check+i)+j)=1;
		 }
	 }
	find();
	show2();
}

bool find(){
   if(solve(0,0)=='*'){
      cout<<"no path!";
      return false;
   }
   return true;
}

bool solve(int x,int y){
   if(x==row-1&&y==col-1){
      {
	  sol[x][y]='-';
	  s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
	  }
      return true;
   }
   if(valid(x,y)==true){
	   sol[x][y]='-';
      s.push(x);
      s.push(y);
      check[x][y]=0;
  //	  cout<<x<<y<<endl;
  	  
	if(solve(x+1,y)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
	else if(solve(x,y+1)==true)
	{
        return true;
 }
     else if(solve(x,y-1)==true)
     {
	  return true;  
}
    else if(solve(x-1,y)==true)
    {
       return true;
}
   else if(solve(x+1,y+1)==true)
   {
   	return true;
   }
    else{
      sol[x][y]='*';
     check[x][y]=1;
      s.pop();
      s.pop();
      return false;
   }
   return false;
}
}

bool valid(int x,int y){
	//cout<<x<<y<<endl<<data[x][y]<<endl<<input[iter]<<endl;
   if((x>=0 && x<row && y>=0 && y<col ) && (data[x][y]==input[iter] )&& (CheckVisited(check,x,y)==true))
   {
   	    iter++;
		return true;
		
   }
   else
    return false;
}






void show(){
	ofstream f2("output1.txt");
    for(int i=0;i<row;i++){
      for(int j=0;j<col;j++)
      	if(sol[i][j] == '-'){
      		cout<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;      		
      		f2<<"("<<i<<","<<j<<")"<<endl;
		  }
   }
   f2.close();
}
void show2(){
s.show3();
}
06/04/2020, 9:19 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include <iostream>
#define QSize 100
using namespace std;
class Queue {
   
    public:
    int q[QSize];
    int front = -1;
    int last = -1;
    int number = 0;
   
   
    void enqueue(int x)
    {
        if(!isFull())
        {
            last = (last + 1) % QSize;
            // mod operator for wrap-around
            q[last] = x;
            number++;
        }
    }
   

    int dequeue()
    {
        if(!isEmpty())
        {
            front = (front + 1) % QSize;
            int x = q[front];
            number--;
            return x;
        }  

       
       
    }

    bool isEmpty()
    {
        if (number > 0)
            return false;
        else
            return true;
    }

    bool isFull()
    {
        if (number < QSize)
            return false;
        else
            return true;
    }
};
int main()
{
    Queue q;
    q.enqueue(1);
    q.enqueue(2);
    q.enqueue(3);
    q.enqueue(4);
    q.enqueue(5);
    q.enqueue(6);
    q.enqueue(7);
    int arr[7];
    cout<<endl<<"enter time";
    for(int i=0;i<7;i++){
    cin>>arr[i];
	}
    while(arr[0]>0){
    for(int i=0;i<7;i++){
    arr[i]=arr[i]-2;  
	}
    }
    int a=0;
    while(a!=-1){
    if(arr[a]<=0){
    q.dequeue();
    a=a+1;
	}
	else
    a=-1;
}
    for(int i=0;i<7;i++){
    cout<<arr[i]<<" ";
}

}

06/04/2020, 9:58 pm - Mubasher Ansari: #include<iostream>
#define SIZE 7
using namespace std;
class Queue{
	private:
    	int items[SIZE],front,rear;
	public:
   		Queue(){
        front=-1;
        rear=-1;
    }
    bool isFull(){
        if(front==0 && rear==SIZE-1){
            return true;
        }
        if(front==rear+1){
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
    bool isEmpty(){
        if(front==-1) 
		return true;
        else 
		return false;
    }
    void enQueue(int element){
        if(isFull()){
            cout<<"Queue is full";
        }else{
            if(front==-1)
			front=0;
            rear=(rear+1)%SIZE;
            items[rear]=element;
            cout<<endl<<element<<endl;
        }
    }
    int deQueue(){
        int element;
        if(isEmpty()){
            cout<<"Queue is empty"<<endl;
            return(-1);
        }
		else{
            element=items[front];
            if(front==rear){
                front=-1;
                rear=-1;
            } 
            else{
                front=(front+1)%SIZE;
            }
            return(element);
        }
    }
    void display(){
    	int i;
        if(isEmpty()) {
            cout<<endl<<"Empty Queue"<<endl;
        }
        else
        {
            cout<<"Front: "<<front;
            cout<<endl<<"Items: ";
            for(i=front;i!=rear;i=(i+1)%SIZE){
                cout<<items[i]<<"\t";
            }
            cout<<items[i];
        }
    }
};

using namespace std;
class Queue{
	private:

        rear=-1;
    }

        if(front==0 && rear==SIZE-1){
            return true;
        }
        if(front==rear+1){
            return true;
        }
        return false;

			front=0;
